<Review>Just finished up visiting. Dad is a HUGE John Force fan, hes visiting from NY and 1 of the places he wanted to go while out visiting was John Forces museum. As someone else mentioned, museum is $5 bucks but they give u $5 off when u spend $30. Good deal IMHO especially since in the store everything is reasonably priced. That being said the 3 people we dealt with at Racestation today 8/25 in the afternoon were AMAZING. Beyond friendly and courteous. With the amount of Force racing memorabilia in the museum it was worth the $5. Its awe inspiring to see so many of the trophies he won there. But the people here were amazing, knowledgeable and courteous and they put on a good face for the Force organization. It is well worth a stop to view, weather you are a huge fan like my dad is or a casual fan like myself.</Review>< Pics>

< review>
I had a GREAT time at John Force Racing in Yorba Linda, CA. The young guy at the gift shop was terrific and very helpful. The museum area is more than worth the $5.00 admission, (which they give back to you should you buy something in the gift shop). I highly recommend stopping by and seeing the Force shop in Yorba Linda...you will not be disappointed!</review>

Ryan Roter</Name>
<Date>1549977022991< /Date>< rating>
5< /rating>
< Review>
Legitimately my favorite Mexican restaurant in Ventura. As a vegetarian Mexican food can be tough because there is hidden lard in a lot of ingredients. While their refried beans do contain lard (authentic style) they have a whole bean option which does not. Their sour cream does contain gelatin which they were nice enough to research for me. The rice does not contain chicken broth. Tortillas are lard free. The people who work there are friendly and patient, and the service is fast and consistent. They also take phone orders for takeout.

I work nearby and go here once a week or more for a whole bean, rice, and cheese burrito with onions. Make sure to get their red salsa, it's amazingly good. I really hope they start selling it by the bottle because it's addicting. The hours make it a little difficult to try if you don't work nearby enough to swing by before work or on your lunch break, but if you can, you absolutely should.<//Review>

<user>107210457441647616894< /user><Review>Steven, my stylist for eleven years and my colorist for the last three, is brilliant. In all this time, he has consistently delivered the perfect style and color.

Steven patiently talks me through various options, and will offer opinions or follow instructions, or do some combination of both - whatever I ask. I feel safe in his hands because I trust his judgment and impeccable sense of style. He is exceptionally creative and precise.

Steven has executed every kind of hairstyle imaginable with me, at all lengths, as well as highlights of various shades and dimensions. He has done a phenomenal job with both cut and color every time. People always ask me where I get my hair done because he is so awesome.

Of less obvious import, but essential to me, is Steven's presence. He is a smart, hilarious, and kind person. I know for a fact that he won't talk to you if you prefer to sit in the chair in silence, but I never want that. I have fun at my appointments because I get to talk to a high quality person. I can't imagine going to anyone else.

In its current incarnation, Veer & Wander has been around for just a few years, but I didn't notice any turnover when it changed names. As far as I know, they only added people, all of whom I like.

The cosmetics counter came in with the name change. I love it. The people on that side have great ideas, and have taken time trying different products on my face to see what works. I really like shopping in there.

I always love first experiences and since I‚Äôd never been to Thirsty Bay Tap N Pour I‚Äôd say this is another first on the books! The spot is conveniently located near the bar station. I didn‚Äôt plan very well because otherwise I would have taken bart so I didn‚Äôt have too drive. But since we wanted to be here early I drove. It was not hard to find, it‚Äôs co-located or adjoined with apartments above! Totally cool!

The ambiance was nice, not too bright and it‚Äôs dimmed. There are several tables inside which I like because I don‚Äôt like to stand. Love that the beer is self-served, you can choose what you want from 39 different beers on Tap! They give you a wrist band to keep track of what you‚Äôve drank so far Is that not awesome? If you like beer this might be your bar! Oh they also have wine.

I like all kinds of beer, dark, light, cider, name it and I‚Äôll try it. But this time I was drawn to the Hibiscus Cider and Maui Cider. It reminded me of Hawaii. The food was ok. It wasn‚Äôt something I‚Äôve never had. I did like the seasoned fries though! It was a hit!!!

The staff were really nice! I give them 5 stars! Accommodating, attentive, and always smiling! It was a great place to have beer with friends. I was really excited to see the Tap bar self-serve I‚Äôd never seen one before! I‚Äôll have to come back here with some friends!!!< /review>

< Review>
Neat place with a good concept.

If your indecisive person like me, you will like this place. Whenever we go hangout to get some drinks, I never really have a specific beer in mind that I want to get. Thats why I like this place because you can pour your own and try different types until you find the one you like. Prices varies depending on the type of beer. I dont think its that expensive. They serve wine and some food too but we didn't get a chance to try it. This place is worth cheking out and it is conveniently located close to Bart. So if you happen to be in Dublin area you should check this place out.< /Review>

<Pictures>None< /Pictures>< Review>
This is perfect for anyone who loves craft beer and indecisive beer drinkers. It's a tap and pour style bar where you pour the beer yourself in a glass of your choice. It's perfectly acceptable to taste every beer they have in stock without getting "the look" from the bar tender for not being able to decide on a drink after a few sample tastings. If beer isn't your thing they also have Wine and Cider on tap for you to pour! Their food menu has a few typical bar staples like wings and onion rings, since opening they've expanded their menu to include pizzas  like zucchini fries! The staff is also very friendly and are eager to help answer any questions. This place is a personal favorite.< /Review>

I like the inside, very colorful with art everywhere! Small menu but I'm sure it's because everything is delicious. Had a Chile relleno burrito and I enjoyed every last bite. I put some of the red wet burrito sauce on it because why not! My girlfriend said her wet burrito was also very delicious and would definitely try the the green one next time. They have a small salsa bar with all you can eat chips so that is a plus. Got the 2 meals and 3 small horchatas for $20 and some change. Overall very nice place to eat only thing that sucks is there was no parking, and it wasn't packed they just obviously don't have restaurant parking since its in a ghetto neighborhood.</review>

< text>
Great prices on grocery provided to you by cutting labor on following : 25c deposit for (you to unlock and return )shopping cart.  You bag your own groceries. Dont mind offbrands. I live for their Crofton cooking implements and appliances. Reasonably priced items and high quality at the same time. Items in the store are usually  fresh - they have high turnover because the small quantities on the shelf are restocked regularly. < Review>
I love shopping here. It's our new go-to grocery store, even though it's a lot father away from us. Overall their prices are cheaper than everywhere else.

In order to lower prices, they have a few things that they do differently to save money, & pass on the savings to customers. For example, you have to bag your own groceries. Also, you have to pay a quarter to get a shopping cart, but you get your quarter back when you return the cart. Don't forget to bring a quarter so you don't have to ask the cashier for one.

It's smaller than the major grocery store, but bigger than Trader Joe's. Instead of a massive selection, of a variety of brands & sizes, there are fewer options, but again, cheaper. Because of this, the shopping process is a lot quicker & easier than wading through a large store.

It's clean & well organized.< /Review>
